0(): / 'tsha nan mnananas nar nan/ rnam
1(): pU ra k+Sha ra ba dz+wa yA na ta n+tu se na ra d+hA pu sti kA sti/
2(): snga 'gyur rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud sde rin po che'i glegs pam bzhugs so//
1a1(1): / h+la r+b+ha //
1a2(1): ma ta
1a3(1): ma mo rtsa ba'i rgyud 'bum tig gi skor bzhugs so// /
1b1(1): thugs kyi yang mying ma mo 'bum tig gi rgyung / bcom ldan 'das pa' la he ru ka rtag pa
1b2(1): chen po la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems khyab gdal ba'i rang bzhin la/ yum las dngos grub chen por bstan pa dang / thugs
1b3(1): kyi sgrom bu las byung ba'i// dgongs pa'i gnag pa mthar phyin pa'i don du gsungs pa las/ gnod 'dul lha yis yang gsol pa// 'jig
1b4(1): rten pa'i chos rnams las// sems nyid ji ltar mya ngan 'da'// rtag chad rnam gnyis gang du bsdu// yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsol
1b5(1): gcig/ de skad gsol ba gsan nas kyang // nyi ga gcig yab kyis bka' stsal pa// nyon gcig g.yung drung yang dag pa// snod kyi
2a1(1): 'jig rten kun bzang // bcud kyi 'jig rten sangs rgyas rgyu// phyi nang snod bcud rnam par dag
2a2(1): rtag chad rnam gnyis mya ngan 'das// g.yung drung lha yi yang gsol pa// ston pa rnam gsum gang la bgyi// sdud pa rnam gsum gang la bgyi//
2a3(1): gnas zhes bgyi ba ji lta bu// gnas la nges pa du zhig mchis// dus zhes bya ba ji lta bu// dus la nges pa du zhig mchis// yang dag
2a4(1): rdzogs kyi bka' stsol cig/ de skad gsol pa gsan nas kyang // yang rag rdzogs kyi bka' stsal pa// nyon cig g.yung drung yang dag pa//
2a5(1): ston pa rnam gsum ye shes sku// sdud pa rnam gsum rig pa'i gter// 'pho 'gyur med pas gnas zhes bya// yang dag don rtogs dus
2b1(1): zhes bya// rdo rje sems dpas yang gsol ba// lha la rnam pa du zhig mchis// 'khor la rnam pa du zhig mchis// lung la rnam pa du zhig mchis// yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsol
2b2(1): cig/ de skad gsol bgasan nas kyang // yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsol ba// nyon cig g.yung drung yang dag pa// lha la rnam pa gsum du bstan// 'khor la rnam pa gsum du
2b3(1): bstan// lung la rnam pa gsum du bstan// rdo rje sems dpas yang gsol ba// rgyu ces bya ba ji ltar lags// lung zhes bgyi ba ji ltar lags// mnangs bgyi ba ji ltar la//
2b4(1): de skad gsol pa gas na nas kyang // yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsal pa// nyon cig g.yung drung yang dag pa// rgyud ces bya ba 'brel pa'i bka'// lus zhes bya ba ston pa'i
2b5(1): bka'// man ngag ces bya ba la zla'o// g.yung drung lha'i yang gsol pa// yum gyi dbyings shes gang la bgyi// yab kyi mkha' shes gang la bgyi// glang dor med pa gang gis
2b6(1): bsgrub// 'khor ba'i gnas 'di ma 'tshal na// klong zhes bya ba ji ltar lags// de skad gsol ba gas na nas kyang // yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsal pa// nyon cig
3a1(1): g.yung drung yang dag pa// 'du 'bral med pa yum gyi dbyings// skye shi med pa yab kyi mkha'// blang ngor med pa bde chen grong // bde ba chen po'i don
3a2(1): rtogs na// blang ngor med pa de yis 'grub// gnyis med don rtogs de'i ngang // rdo rje sems dpas yad gsol ba// chos nyid zag pa'i g.yung drub ga// sems nyid rtogs pa'i
3a3(1): blos bzhag na// 'gyur med don zhes rung lags sam// yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsal pa// nyon cig g.yung drung yang dag pa// chos nyid rtag pa'i g.yung drung la// sems
3a4(1): nyid rtag pa'i bro bzhag pa// rdzogs pa'i lta bar la dor ro// rdo rje sems dpas yang gsol pa// ma zhes bya ba gang gi dbyings// mo zhes bya ba gang gi klong // ma mo'i gtan tshigs
3a5(1): ji ltar lags// 'byung ba lnga po gang las grub// sangs rgyas dgongs pa gang gis 'grub/ bde ba chen po'i rang nyid las// rgyu rkyen gnyis kyi bskyed lags sam/
3a6(1): 'byung ba lnga yi rang nyid las// 'di la 'pho 'gyur mchis lags sam// yang dag rdzogs kyi bka' stsal pa// nyon cig g.yung drung yang dag pa// ma mo'i don rnams rtogs pa ni//
3b1(1): ma mo'i sa rnams nges par thob// yid bzhin nor bum btsal rnyed// ye shes nyi ma rangal shar// chen po lnga'i ngang nyid du// thams cad ma lus sangs rgyas so// gsang pa gtan tshig gi le'u ste dang po'o//
3b2(1): gnod 'dul lha yi yang gsol pa// theg padaman pa'i 'og ma dang // skye bo dam med dam nyams la// mi stan sba ba'i dam tshig gang // bdag gis nan tan ji ltar bgyi// mngon sangs rgyas la bdag nyan 'tshal/
3b3(1): mngon sangs rgyas kyi bka' stsol cig/ de skad gsol ba gsan nas kyang // mngon sangs rgyas kyi bka' stsal pa// theg pa dman pa'i 'og ma dang // skye bo dam med dam nyams pa// mi bstan pa'i dam tshig ni/
3b4(1): the tshom med par nges stan gyi// ngas gsungs pa la rtse gcig sems bskyed cig/ theg pa 'og ma rnams la gsang ba ni// rtog pa'i lta ba chen po gsang // mdzod spyod ngo mtshar chen po gsang // rdo rje slob
3b5(1): dpon bsgrub rog gsang // ma mo bstan pa'i dam rdzas gsang // bsgrub par byed pa'i lag cha gsang // bzlas par bya ba'i sngags rnams gsang // bsgrub pa'i gnas kyang de bzhin no// bsgrub pa'i dus
3b6(1): kyang de bzhin no// bsgrub pa'i rtags kyang de bzhin no// dngos grub rtags kyang ba lnga ma bzhin// blang ba'i thabs kyang gsang bar bya// dbang du bsdu ba'i thabs kyang rab tu gsad// bkol ba'i thabs kyang de bzhin//
3b7(1): gdams pa'i gsang pa'i dam tshig ni// gdams pa bzhin du mnyan te// gsang ba mthub 'bras bu ni// til 'bru tsam yang thob mi 'gyur// dngos grub nyid kyang ring ba dang // de ni rigs kyang yod mi
4a1(1): byed// ces bka' stsal to// man dag dam tshig gi le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / gnod 'phrul lnga yis yang gsol ba// rnal 'byor zab mo 'don spyod la// lta ba'i don gyis
4a2(1): phan gdags pa// bdag gis nan tan ji ltar bskyed// rtag chen yab la bdag nyan 'tshal// rtag chen yab kyi bka' stsol cig/ de skad gsol pa gsan nas kyang // rtag chen yab kyi bka' stsal ba// rnal 'byor zab mo'i
4a3(1): don spyod la// lta ba'i don gyis phan gdags pa// yang dag nyid du ngas bstan gyis// nyon cig g.yung drung lha'i gtso// nges bstan pa la the mtshem med// gnod kyi 'jig rten shes bya'i yul// bcud kyi 'jig rten rig
4a4(1): pa ste// yul dang gnyis med don gyi lta bar bya// ma mo mkha' 'gro skyabs dang grogs su lta// snod kyis 'jig rten chos kyi dbyings// bcud kyi rten ye shes che// dbyings dang ye shes gnyis med don gyi blta// thabs
4a5(1): dang shes rab 'du 'bral med par blta// yab yub rol pa byang chub sems su blta// ma mo mkha' 'gro bran dang g.yog du blta// sprul pa sna tshogs 'phro 'du dbyings su blta// snang srid thams cad byang chub sems
4a6(1): kyi thig ler blta// snod kyi 'jig rten byang chub sems// bcud kyi 'jig rten ye shes klong // gnyis med don gyi skye med sku ru blta// ma mo mkha' 'gro byang chub sems kyi sprul par lnga// snang srid thams cad thig
4a7(1): le chen por blta// snod bcung gnyis med rtag chen ga yung drung sku// snang srid gnyis med ye shes thig le'i klong // 'phro 'du thams cad sems kyi 'bras bu ste// ma mo mkha' 'gro ye shes 'phro 'du blta/
4b1(1): lung 'di nyid kyi lta ba ni// ma Ni skye med sgra/ ru blta// mo ni brjod med gsung du blta// ma dang mo ni gnyis med thugs su blta// ma ni byang chub sems su blta// ma ni ye shes klong du blta// gnyis med rtogs pa chen
4b2(1): bor blta// ma ni skye med rnam dag dbyings// mo ni 'gyur med ye shes te// gnyis med rtag pa'i g.yung drung sku// ma dang mo'i ngang nyid ni// gnyis su med pa'i byang chub sems// ma dang mo yi ngang nyid ni// ye nas
4b3(1): gnyis med chos kyi sku// ma dang mo'i ngang nyid ni// ye nas rdo rje snying por blta// ma dang mo yi ngang nyid las// ye nas 'bras bu gsum du blta// ma ngang mo yi rang nyid ni// ye nas stong pa gsum du blta// ma dang ma
4b4(1): yi rang nyid ni// rtogs na rgyal ba'i sku yang yin// ma rtogs dmyal ba'i gnas su 'gro// mdor na ma dang mo yi rang nyid ni// 'tsho bar byed pa'i sman yang yin// 'chi bar byed pa'i dug kyang yin// ces bca' stsal
4b5(1): ba dang / 'khor rnams ngam nas ya mtshan skyes so// ma mo blta ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// gnod 'dul lha yi yang gsol ba// sems can rnams la phan gdags phyir// bsgoms pa'i don
4b6(1): la bdag nyan 'tshal// yang dog rdzogs kyi bka' stsol cig/ de skad gsol ba gsan nas kyang // mngon rdzogs rgyal pos bka' stsal ba// bsgom pa'i don 'dings bstan gyis// nyon cig g.yung drung
4b7(1): yang dag pa// ngas gsung ba la sems ma yengs// de la dang po de bzhin nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin ni// srang srid thams cad ma byung ma skyes par bsgom// de nas kun tu snang gi ting nge 'dzin ni// snying rje nam mkha'i ra ba
5a1(1): ltar// snang la rang bzhin med par sgom// de nas rgyu'i ting nge 'dzin ni// oM dkar po bkra sa le sgom// oM de las 'od 'phros pas/ 'phags pa'i thugs kyi rgyud bskul// 'gro ba sems can
5a2(1): gyi don bris nas/ slar 'dus pa las/ ye shes lngar gyur par bsgom mo// ye shes lnga'i 'od zer las/ e taM maM su ka byaM b+h+rUM/ zhes brjod pas/ yi ge de rnams rin chen gtsar la rgyas pa bzhin// dkar khrigs so
5a3(1): bsgom// de na e b+ha ga ba pad+ma maN+Dal zhes brjod pas/ yi ge e las gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang ldan pa gcig tu gyur nas/ snang srid kun la khyab par bsgom mo// de'i byin rlabs las 'og gi phyogs su ta taM zhes
5a4(1): brjod pas/ rlung gi tshub ma la rdo rje rgya gram gyi kha bcang par bsgom mo// de'i steng du maM las rak+ta maN+Dal zhes brjod pas/ rak+ta'i rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med pa/ dmar tshil bar gyur par bsgom mo// de'i steng du
5a5(1): su las badz+ra sum zhes brjod pas/ gser gyi sa gzhi/ dper na mtsho la dar chags pa tsam mam/ 'o ma la spri ma chags pa'i tshul du skad kyi chags par bsgom mo// de'i steng du keng las keng ni ri dz+wa la maN+Dal zhes
5a6(1): brjod pas// keng rus kyi ri rab gsar snying brtsegs pa la/ gnam lcags kyi rdo rje rtse gcig pa'i gzer gyi btab pas/ rtsibs la nyi zla 'char ba bsgom mo// de'i steng du phyi las ag+na maN+Dal ces brjod pas
5a7(1): 'byung ba me'i dkyil 'khor gyis// 'byung ba thams cad cha snyam te// gro'i rlung langs pa bzhin myal gyis btang bar bsgom mo// de'i steng du sum las su badz+ra sum me zhes brjod pas/ ri rab rin po che sna lnga las
5b1(1): grub/ shar shel ka ka ri ltar dkar ba/ lhobai DUr+ya ltar sngo ba/ nub pad+ma ra ga ltar dmar ba// byang in+d+ra ne le ltar ldang ba/ dbus su sha ra ka ltar ser ba/ dpag tshad brgyad khri bzhi stong du byin pa
5b2(1): kha khyer gyen du byung bas/ nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched 'phang bcad par bsgom mo// de'i steng dum dmar mo gcig gsal nas/ de'i steng du b+h+yo smug nag gcig bsgom mo// de las 'od zer 'phros pas/ 'phags
5b3(1): pa'i thugs dam gyi rgyud bkul// 'gro ba sems can gyi don byas nas slar 'dus pa las// b+hA bi shrA bi shu d+ha dz+nyA na tsakra ban+d+ha dz+dza/ zhes brjod pas/ ye shes kyi gzhal yas khang gru ba'i sgo bzhi pa dang ldan pa/
5b4(1): sgo 'khyud lta bab dang ldan pa gcig tu gyur par bsgom mo// gzhal yas khang de'i nang du dur khrod kyi brgyan mang pos brgyan par bsgom mo// de'i steng du ma dmar mo gcig gsal bar bsgom mo// de la sa ma
5b5(1): sur+ya mnal zhes brjod pa sa/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor du gyur pa ra bsgom mo// de'i steng du a kar po gcig gsal ba las/ a tsaN+Da maN+Dal zhes brjod pas/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor du gyur par bsgom mo//
5b6(1): nyi zla'i steng du tsakra maN+Dal zhes brjod pas/ 'khor lo rtsibs bzhi pa gcig tu gyur pa bsgom mo// de'i steng du ma hA de wa pho mo bsgom mo// ma hA de wa u ma de wa kha tsA kha ster ba zhes brjod pas/ dbang phyug chen
5b7(1): po gan rkyal du bsgyel nas gnas gdan du bting ba rab sgom mo// de'i steng du g+hu'i yi ge/ oM dkar po bkra saM le bsgom mo// oM de las 'od zer 'phros 'dus pa las/ byang chub sems su gyur par
6a1(1): bam so// de yang sdang srid sa mo tsam yang / ma g.yos pa'i thig le gsal bar bsgom mo// thig le de las/ oM gro ya dAn+ta hrI/ be nukab+hUM/ zhes tha med cer
6a2(1): ka'i skur gsal gyi gyur to// ting nge 'dzin gyis lcogs tshad du dgu dbu// phyag bco brgyad par bsgom mo// de ltar mi gsal na sku mdog mthing nag la// g.yas dka re g.yon dmar/ dbu gsum
6a3(1): phyag drug pa zhabs pa ni phyogs bzhir gtams par bsgom mo// gshog pa phyogs bzhir brkyang ba// glang po che'i ko rlon gyi stong g.yog dang / ning lpags kyi g.yang gzhi dang / zod rnon gyi phreng ba tshar gas
6a4(1): gyi sa brgyan pa// dbu rgyan mgur chu do shal byas/ klu rigs bzhis sku la brgyan pa// mtshan ma rnam pa gsum gyis mtshan pa/ stag lpags kyi sham thabs kyis rgyan pa/ zhal g.yas dkar ba g.yon
6a5(1): dmar ba// dbus sku dang mthun te mthong nag/ phyag g.yas dang po na rdo rje rtse dgu pa thogs pa// g.yas par man ral gribasnams pa// g.yas tha ma ma zhags pa bsnam pa/ g.yon dang pon dril bu bsnams
6a6(1): pa/ g.yon par ma na rnge'u/ g.yon tha ma na dgra lta bsnams par bsgom mo// de ltar gsal ba dang / g.yon gyi phyogs su gu ya kro d+hi shwa ri hUM zhes brjod pas/ lus la dri ba ma byung ba'i tshul du/ yuH
6a7(1): nyid gsang ba'i yum chen mo ragasal gyis gyur par bsgom mo// sku mdog dang phyag cha gtso dang mthun par bsgom mo// zhal lnga phyag drug pa'o// g.yas dang pon dril bu bsnams pa/ g.yon dang po
6b1(1): na b+han+d+ha rak+ta sa bkang ba thogs pa/ g.yas pa ra ma na zhags pa thogs pa/ g.ya sa tha man bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga thogs pa/ g.yon dang po bcu ltag sprod kyi rnga bsnams pa/ g.yon tha ma nag yang gzhi bsnam
6b2(1): ba/ zhabs rnam pa brgyad dang ldan pa gcig gsal bar bsgom mo// de nas yab yum gnyis su med pa'i brdas bskul nas/ sbyor ba mdzad nas byang chub sems 'od zer 'phros pa sa lcags kyus
6b3(1): srid pa yis/ ma mo ku na bku ga na se ga dan bting / dza hUM baM hoHkro d+hI shA ri sti ri baM shin+na ri baM/ mu tri ti ri baM/ shan+ti sti ra baM/ dun+d+hi ti ra bau/ dun+ti sti ra baM// su r+ya ti ra baM/ pad+ma sti rA baM/
6b4(1): kha ra ka bi sti tir baM/ sr-id gro ti ra baM/ badz+ra kre k+Sho sti ra baM/ badz+ro ta kr-i badz+ra te kr-i sta~M ra ba~M/ badz+ra ni la badz+ra ni la/ s+thi ra baM/ badz+ra lin+d+ra badz+ra lan+d+ha stir baM/ nan zhes brjod pas/ gan rgyal du ling ling
6b5(1): 'gyel nas/ phyogs phyogs su gdan du gting bar bsgom mo// yang yab yum gnyis su med pa'i byang chub kyi sems las/ yi ge he rer gsal bar bsgom mo// yi ge ha 'phros 'dus
6b6(1): pa las/ byang chub sems su gyur par bsgom mo// shar phyogs 'khor lo'i rtsibs stengs su/ sgrol byed ma dang dkar mo mig gcig ma gnyis bsnol ba'i gdan stengs su/ byang chub kyi
6b7(1): sems yi go ha las/ oM g+ha swa mu ma hA d+hig ce sa brjod pas/ rtag pa'i rgyal mo rnam snang gsal gyis skor bsal gyis gyur to// skra mdog dkar mo la/ dbu gsum phyag drug par bsgom mo// g.yas
7a1(1): dang po rdo rje ba ra ba na sgra sta/ tha ma na seng ge bsnams pa/ g.yon dang po bat+tA rak+Shas bkang ba/ bar man bdun shing / rdeg pa'i tshul ston pa/ tha ma na mchog chen spong bar
7a2(1): bsgom ma// zhabs bzhi pargyung bskum du bzhugs par bsgom mo// byang phyogs 'khor lo'i rtsibs stengs su/ dbang phyugs dang ral gcig ma gnyis bsnol ba'i bden stengs su/ byang chub kyi
7a3(1): sems yi ge ha las/ oM bying yong yang ti ha d+h+ri ga ces brjod pas/ mkha' 'gro ma yang gsal g.yos sgyur gsal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog ljang khu la dbu gsum phyag drug par gyur to//
7a4(1): phyag ga las dang ba rdo rje rgya gra ma bsnams pa/ g.yas bar ma na dbyug/ chen po bsnams pa/ g.yas tha ma na sbyang mo bsnams po/ g.yon dang po na ban+de bsnams pa/ g.yon par man rgyu 'phyang bsnam
7a5(1): / g.yon tha ma na zhing chung bzung zhing bsnams/ spyod par bsgom mo// zhabs bzhi brkyang bskum du bzhugs par bsgom mo// nub phyogs 'khor lo'i rtsibs stengs su/ bdud rtsi po
7a6(1): dmar mo gnyis bsngal po'i bdas snyed s+yA s+t+wa~M/ byang chub sems laM ge ha las/ oM d+hI sha sa~Md+g+ha na~M d+h+r-iH kyis brjod pa sa/ gakha' 'gros gnyen bsal ma sal gyis gyur te/ sgyu mngag dmar
7a7(1): mal zhal gsum phyag drug par gyur to// phyag g.yas dang po na bad+ma bsnams pa/ bar na zhags pa/ tha ma na lce spyang 'dzin pa/ g.yon dang po na ban+d+ha bsnams pa/ ba ra man tri shul bsnga
7b1(1): ga/ tha ma na zhing chen thogs nas spyod par bsgom mo// lho phyogs 'khor lo'i rtsibs stengs su/ dbang sdud ma dang ma ral gcig ma gnyis bsnol ba'i gangan stengs su/ byang chub sems yi
7b2(1): ge ha las/ oM badz+ra la raM ha d+h+rig ces brjod pas/ mkha' 'gro 'od gsal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog sngon mo la zhal gsum phyag drug par bsgom mo// phyag g.yas dang po na rin po che 'bar
7b3(1): ba bsnams pa/ tha ma nA sdug mo 'dzin pa/ g.yon dang po na ban+d+ha/ ba ra ma na dbyug to bar ba/ tha ma na zhing chung baM bo bzung nas stong bar bsgom mo// zhabs bzhi brgyad bskum du bzhugs par
7b4(1): bsgom mo// 'khor lo'i ste ba'i dbus kyi dkyilan/ dpal chen po sgoms pa'i g.yas phyogs su/ ma mo 'phra men ma rgya mtsho dang / nyi zla thod phreng ma gnyis bsnol ba'i gongan stengs su/ byang
7b5(1): chub kyi sems yi ge ha las/ oM ma hUM la te ha d+hI ce sa brjod pas/ yuM bkrag gsal mar sal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog ser mo la zhal gsum phyag drug par bsgom mo// zhal g.yas dkar
7b6(1): ga g.yon dmar ba/ dbus ser bya/ g.ya sa dang blon 'khor lo bsnams pa/ bAr+ya ma nA rgyal mtshan/ b+hU man drug pa 'dzin pa/ g.yon dang po nI ban+d+ha/ bya ra man spu gri bsnams pa/ tha ma
7b7(1): na zhing chung gzung nas spod par bsgom mo// zhabs bzhi brkyang sbrum du bzhugs par bsgom mo// de nas bdag nyid dpal chen po'i thugs kar/ rin po che smug po gur thub pa 'dra ba'i nang na/ dngas
8a1(1): ma zhi zhig yod de/ rtsa'i dngas ma dang khrag gi dngas ma dang / dbugs kyi dngas ma dang / 'od kyi dngas ma dang bzhi las/ shar lho'i mtshams su rgyan gyi rgya la mo bskyed pa'i gdan
8a2(1): skyengs su/ rtsa'i dngas ma las/ A~M ka ma la shA ri ha d+h+r-ig ces brjod pas/ gsang ba'i yum rgyas 'debs mar gsal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog mar skya la/ sku phyag gis gang po/ zhal spyan
8a3(1): gyis gang ba gcig bsgom mo// lho nub tu dbyings phyug ma skyed pa'i gdan stengs su/ khra ga gi dwang sa ma la sa/ AM ka ma la shA ri ha d+hI ga/ ces brjod pa sa gsang ba'i yum za byed ma'i sku ro
8a4(1): gsal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog mthing nag la/ sku dbugs kyis gang ba/ phyag gis gang ba gcig bsgom mo// nub byang bdud rtsi'am bskyed pa'i gdan stengs su/ dbug sA kyis dngos
8a5(1): ma las/ oM ka ma la shwa ri ha d+h+ri gA ces brjod pas/ yu mA rmongs byed mar sal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog dmar mo laM/ sku lus khrag gis gong ba/ phyag rlung gis grang ba gcig bsgom mo//
8a6(1): byang shar du gcig pu ma bskyed pa'i gdan stengs su/ 'od kyi dngas mo las/ oM ka ma la shwa ri had+h+r-i ga ces brjod pas/ yu ma tshe 'phel mar sal gyis gyur te/ sku mdog ldang chu
8a7(1): la/ sku bad kan gyi gang po/ phyag chu ser gyis gang bar gyur te/ de ltar gsal ba dang / byang chub sems las 'od zer 'phros 'dus pa las/ dza hUM ba~M ho// ma ma b+h+yo pha Ta nan//
8b1(1): mam du Sha na phaTanan/ ma ma tra ga ragra pra we sha phaT nan/ shan nan ti ra baM ces brjod pas/ srid pa'i dbang chen rnams/ kha bu ba gan rgyal du brgyal bar bsgom mo// yang byang chub sems
